Accessibility test digest

Synopsis

Page: Railpass

URL: https://www.railpass.com/

Score: 1105

Tested by: Testaro, procedure tp10

Scored by: Testilo, procedure sp10b

Digested by: Testilo, procedure dp10b

Introduction

The tp10 accessibility testing procedure was executed by Testaro on the Railpass web page at https://www.railpass.com/, on 2022/06/03. The procedure performed 808 tests. Of these, 16 tests are custom tests defined by Testaro, and the others belong to packages of tests created by others. Testaro produced a report enumerating the test results.

Testilo used its sp10b scoring procedure to compute partial and total scores for the page. The total score is 1105 (where 0 is the best possible score). The scored report is appended below.

Finally, Testilo used procedure dp10b to produce this digest, explaining how sp10b computed the scores.

Disclaimer: Even though there are widely accepted accessibility standards, there is still no unanimity about how to define, test for, and quantify accessibility. The failures reported below merit investigation as potential opportunities for improved accessibility. But you may conclude that some of the failures do not actually harm accessibility, and some substantial accessibility faults can escape detection by any of these tests. Likewise, you may not agree with weightings and formulas of scoring procedure sp10b, or even question whether it is appropriate to assign accessibility scores to a web page. This digest describes only one interpretation of the page’s accessibility.

Issue summary

Special issues

log: Score 34. This is based on the amount of browser logging during the tests. Browsers usually log messages only when pages contain erroneous code.

log: Score 36. This is based on issues reported by unclassified tests. Details are in the report.

Classified issues

The classified issues reported by tests are summarized below.

focusIndication: Score undefined. Issues reported by tests in this category:

  • 106 issues reported by package testaro, test focInd (operable elements that cannot be Tab-focused and vice versa)

spontaneousMotion: Score undefined. Issues reported by tests in this category:

  • 74 issues reported by package testaro, test motion (change of visible content not requested by user)

contrastAA: Score undefined. Issues reported by tests in this category:

  • 22 issues reported by package alfa, test r69 (Text outside widget has minimum contrast)
  • 6 issues reported by package axe, test color-contrast (Elements must have sufficient color contrast)
  • 0 issues reported by package ibm, test v:IBMA_Color_Contrast_WCAG2AA (contrast ratio of text with background must meet WCAG 2.1 AA)
  • 22 issues reported by package wave, test c:contrast (Very low contrast)

nameValue: Score undefined. Issues reported by tests in this category:

  • 5 issues reported by package aatt, test e:F68 (Form control wrongly labeled or unlabeled)
  • 16 issues reported by package aatt, test e:H91 (Missing name or value of form control or link)
  • 7 issues reported by package wave, test e:label_missing (Missing form label)

linkNoText: Score undefined. Issues reported by tests in this category:

  • 4 issues reported by package alfa, test r11 (link does not have an accessible name)
  • 4 issues reported by package axe, test link-name (Links must have discernible text)
  • 0 issues reported by package ibm, test v:WCAG20_A_HasText (Hyperlinks must have a text description)
  • 5 issues reported by package tenon, test 57 (This link has no text inside it)

buttonNoText: Score undefined. Issues reported by tests in this category:

  • 0 issues reported by package alfa, test r12 (button does not have an accessible name)
  • 0 issues reported by package axe, test aria-command-name (ARIA commands must have an accessible name)
  • 8 issues reported by package wave, test e:button_empty (Empty button)

inconsistentStyles: Score undefined. Issues reported by tests in this category:

  • 35 issues reported by package testaro, test styleDiff (heading, link, and button style inconsistencies)

contrastAAA: Score undefined. Issues reported by tests in this category:

  • 28 issues reported by package alfa, test r66 (Text contrast less than AAA requires)
  • 8 issues reported by package tenon, test 95 (This element has insufficient color contrast (Level AAA))

focusableOperable: Score undefined. Issues reported by tests in this category:

  • 9 issues reported by package testaro, test focOp (operable elements that cannot be Tab-focused and vice versa)

targetSize: Score undefined. Issues reported by tests in this category:

  • 12 issues reported by package tenon, test 152 (This actionable element is smaller than the minimum required size)

inlineBackgroundRisk: Score undefined. Issues reported by tests in this category:

  • 25 issues reported by package aatt, test w:F24 (Inline background color needs complementary foreground color)

linkUnderlines: Score undefined. Issues reported by tests in this category:

  • 10 issues reported by package testaro, test linkUl (non-underlined inline links)

headingStruc: Score undefined. Issues reported by tests in this category:

  • 4 issues reported by package aatt, test w:G141 (heading structure is not logically nested)
  • 4 issues reported by package alfa, test r53 (heading skips one or more levels)
  • 4 issues reported by package axe, test heading-order (Heading levels should only increase by one)
  • 4 issues reported by package wave, test a:heading_skipped (Skipped heading level)
  • 1 issues reported by package tenon, test 155 (These headings are not structured in a hierarchical manner)

imgNoText: Score undefined. Issues reported by tests in this category:

  • 2 issues reported by package aatt, test e:H37 (Img element missing an alt attribute)
  • 0 issues reported by package alfa, test r2 (image does not have an accessible name)
  • 0 issues reported by package axe, test image-alt (Images must have alternate text)
  • 0 issues reported by package ibm, test v:WCAG20_Img_HasAlt (Images must have an alt attribute if they convey meaning, or alt='' if decorative)
  • 2 issues reported by package wave, test e:alt_missing (Missing alternative text)

noLeading: Score undefined. Issues reported by tests in this category:

  • 7 issues reported by package alfa, test r73 (Paragraphs of text have sufficient line height)

hoverSurprise: Score undefined. Issues reported by tests in this category:

  • 14 issues reported by package testaro, test hover (content changes caused by hovering)

metaBansZoom: Score undefined. Issues reported by tests in this category:

  • 1 issues reported by package alfa, test r47 (meta element restricts the ability to zoom)
  • 1 issues reported by package axe, test meta-viewport (Zooming and scaling should not be disabled)

roleBad: Score undefined. Issues reported by tests in this category:

  • 0 issues reported by package axe, test aria-allowed-role (ARIA role should be appropriate for the element)
  • 0 issues reported by package ibm, test v:aria_semantics_role (ARIA roles must be valid for the element to which they are assigned)
  • 1 issues reported by package testaro, test role (nonexistent or implicit-overriding role)

tabFocusability: Score undefined. Issues reported by tests in this category:

  • 1 issues reported by package testaro, test focAll (discrepancy between elements that should be and that are Tab-focusable)

pseudoHeadingRisk: Score undefined. Issues reported by tests in this category:

  • 5 issues reported by package aatt, test w:H42 (Heading markup should be used if this content is intended as a heading)

visibleBulk: Score undefined. Issues reported by tests in this category:

  • 1 issues reported by package testaro, test bulk (Count of visible elements as a multiple of 300)
